\DoxyCodeLine{00100\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ This\ reduces\ memory\ usage\ by\ up\ to\ 43\%\ when\ using\ a\ large}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00101\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ array\ of\ libdivide\ dividers\ and\ improves\ performance}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00102\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ by\ up\ to\ 10\%\ because\ of\ reduced\ memory\ bandwidth.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00103\ \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#pragma\ pack(push,\ 1)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{00147\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ Explanation\ of\ the\ "{}more"{}\ field:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00148\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00149\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ *\ Bits\ 0-\/5\ is\ the\ shift\ value\ (for\ shift\ path\ or\ mult\ path).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00150\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ *\ Bit\ 6\ is\ the\ add\ indicator\ for\ mult\ path.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00151\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ *\ Bit\ 7\ is\ set\ if\ the\ divisor\ is\ negative.\ We\ use\ bit\ 7\ as\ the\ negative}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00152\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ divisor\ indicator\ so\ that\ we\ can\ efficiently\ use\ sign\ extension\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00153\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ create\ a\ bitmask\ with\ all\ bits\ set\ to\ 1\ (if\ the\ divisor\ is\ negative)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00154\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ or\ 0\ (if\ the\ divisor\ is\ positive).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00155\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00156\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ u32:\ [0-\/4]\ shift\ value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00157\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ [5]\ ignored}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00158\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ [6]\ add\ indicator}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00159\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ magic\ number\ of\ 0\ indicates\ shift\ path}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00160\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00161\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ s32:\ [0-\/4]\ shift\ value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00162\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ [5]\ ignored}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00163\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ [6]\ add\ indicator}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00164\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ [7]\ indicates\ negative\ divisor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00165\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ magic\ number\ of\ 0\ indicates\ shift\ path}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00166\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00167\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ u64:\ [0-\/5]\ shift\ value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00168\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ [6]\ add\ indicator}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00169\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ magic\ number\ of\ 0\ indicates\ shift\ path}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00170\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00171\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ s64:\ [0-\/5]\ shift\ value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00172\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ [6]\ add\ indicator}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00173\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ [7]\ indicates\ negative\ divisor}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00174\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ \ \ \ \ \ magic\ number\ of\ 0\ indicates\ shift\ path}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00175\ \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00176\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ In\ s32\ and\ s64\ branchfree\ modes,\ the\ magic\ number\ is\ negated\ according\ to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00177\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ whether\ the\ divisor\ is\ negated.\ In\ branchfree\ strategy,\ it\ is\ not\ negated.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{00178\ }

\DoxyCodeLine{01925\ \ \ \ \ uint32\_t\ is\_power\_of\_2\ =\ (\mbox{\hyperlink{namespacepandas_1_1io_1_1sas_1_1sas__constants_a9deb025d68bf533abd3c0c0f1c3dfc6d}{magic}}\ ==\ 0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01926\ \ \ \ \ \_\_m128i\ q\_sign\ =\ libdivide\_s64\_signbits(q);\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ q\_sign\ =\ q\ >>\ 63}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01927\ \ \ \ \ \_\_m128i\ mask\ =\ \_mm\_set1\_epi64x((1ULL\ <<\ shift)\ -\/\ is\_power\_of\_2);}
\DoxyCodeLine{01928\ \ \ \ \ q\ =\ \_mm\_add\_epi64(q,\ \_mm\_and\_si128(q\_sign,\ mask));\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ q\ =\ q\ +\ (q\_sign\ \&\ mask)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01929\ \ \ \ \ q\ =\ libdivide\_s64\_shift\_right\_vector(q,\ shift);\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ q\ >>=\ shift}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01930\ \ \ \ \ q\ =\ \_mm\_sub\_epi64(\_mm\_xor\_si128(q,\ sign),\ sign);\ \textcolor{comment}{//\ q\ =\ (q\ \string^\ sign)\ -\/\ sign}}
\DoxyCodeLine{01931\ \ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordflow}{return}\ q;}
